1b1(rgyud 'grel): bcom ldan 'das dpal kun tu bzang po la phyag
1b2(rgyud 'grel): 'tshal lo// mnyam nyid dbyings su bdud bzhi ngang gis bcom/ 
1b3(rgyud 'grel): phyag rgya'i rang bzhin gnyis med rdzogs par ldan// yod med mtha' 
1b4(rgyud 'grel): 'das bdag gzhan yongs kyi dpal// thams cad rang bzhin rtogs 
1b5(rgyud 'grel): dang thugs rje bzang // kun bzang lha'i lha khyod dbyer med la// rtogs dang 
2a1(rgyud 'grel): kyang grus sa du rung rgya sa sa sa ba sa bya chu ba ngas byas bya 
2a2(rgyud 'grel): grub pas rab tu phyag 'tshal lo// gang zhig sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i rgyud 'di nyid// don rtogs gsapa 
2a3(rgyud 'grel): bar bya phyir bdag gis ni// don bsdus rab tu dbye ba 'di brtsam pas// dngos grub mchog gnyis thob par bya phyir 
2a4(rgyud 'grel): bshad// gang gis rgyud 'di rtogs dka' bas// bde rlag du ni rtogs par 'gyur// 'di yi rang bzhin che ba dang / 
2a5(rgyud 'grel): mtshan nyid dang ni don bstan phyir// sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i rgyud chen las// mdor bsdus bstan la phab pa yin// rang bzhin 
2a6(rgyud 'grel): gsang ba zhes bya ste// che ba zhes ni snying pa'i don// de kho na nyid mtshan nyid do// nges pas nges don mdor bstan pa/ 
2a7(rgyud 'grel): de ltar rnam pa bzhi por// mdor bsdus spyi'i don du bshad// rang bzhin gapa dang rgas pa dang // bstan min zhes 
2a8(rgyud 'grel): rgyu rgyu rgyan tu du du tu du rgyu du bya du du ra 
2b1(rgyud 'grel): bya'i rang bzhin ni// mnyam pa nyid dang dgongs pa'i don// mdzad spyod gsang ba'i theg pa nyid// rnam bzhi gsang ba zhes pa'i mtshan// sde gnod rgyud kun 'byung byir dang // bstan la 'bebs dang khyad par che// / 
2b2(rgyud 'grel): ston pa 'khor dang gnas las sogs// mchog tu gyur pas che ba bshad// rgya dang 'bras bu dbyer med pa// don dam kun rdzob gnyis med ni// mtshan nyid zhes bya rnam pa gsum// lus dang man ngag nges pa yang // 
2b3(rgyud 'grel): nges pa'i dbyings nas phyung bas na// nges don don na bstan pa yin// nges don spyi'i mtshan nyid ni// so so rnam grangs don rnams kyi// sngon du 'gro ba'i bdag nyid pas// ming nyid thog mar smos pa gces// rgyu dang rkyen 
2b4(rgyud 'grel): dang gzhung nyid dang // 'gro ba'i don du snang ba'i phyir// gleng gzhi dang ni gleng spangs te// don dang yongs su gzung ba dang // rnam pa bzhi ni bsdus pa yin// gleng gzhi rnam pa lngar bshad de// gang tshe gang gi gang du bshang // 
2b5(rgyud 'grel): gang la gang gis bsdus pa ste// 'byung ba dus dang ston pa dang // gnas dang 'khor dang sdud pa'o// sgro dang skur bzhi pas na// 'di skad zhes su bshad pa yin// sku gsungs thugs kyis bshad pas na// ma rtogs skyon dang 
2b6(rgyud 'grel): gsung thos skyon// bshad ces pas ni spangs pa yin// bla med 'khor lo bskor ba'i tshe// de tshe dus zhes bya bar grags// ston pa zhes bya ba'i mtshan nyid ni// rang bzhin dang ni mdzad spyod dang // rnal 'byor rnams gnyis ngol 
2b7(rgyud 'grel): snang // byang chub chen po'i rang bzhin dang // chos rnams rol bar longs spyod dang // phyogs dus bde gshegs bdag po dang // chos so cig dang dbyer med pa// ston pa'i rang bzhin rnam pa bzhi// don dam chos kyi sku'i mtshan// 
2b8(rgyud 'grel): mdzad spyod gzugs sku rnam gnyis te// longs spyod rdzogs dang sbrul sku'o// longs spyod sngags kyi bdag po'i tshul// rgyal po rgyal mo yang dag ldan// sprul pa rdul snyed thub pa dang // khro rgyal stsogs pagrangs med yin// 
3a1(rgyud 'grel): bdag po sku'i mtshan nyid dang // zhal dang mtshan dang dpe byad dang // bsam 'das zhabs dang phyag mtshan dang // dbu dang sku dang kha dog dang // rgyal mo'i tshogs dang bzhugs pa'i dpe// bcu dang gsum gyis/ 
3a2(rgyud 'grel): rdzogs par rol// ye shes phyi nang med pa dang // thams cad mnyam par dgongs pa dang // sems dpa' sems par ldan pa dang // bcu drag rgyas btab dpe byad dang // lus dang ngag sems nis 'dus par// de rnyed sku gsung 
3a3(rgyud 'grel): snang ba dang // thabs dang shes rab snang ba dang // ye shes drag dang phyag rgya drag/ rna ma thar sku gsung bas ma yas dang // phung po lnga po'i ngo bo nyid// rgyal ba lnga ru rdzogs sangs rgyas// kun kyang kha dog lnga pa ste// nyi shu rtsa lnga rin chen 
3a4(rgyud 'grel): mdog/ snang bar mnyen dro bskyod dang lnga// dbyings kyi ngo bo rgyal po ste// de bzhi na kro te rna ma lnga yin// na mkha' dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa// ston pa'i mdzad spyod rol mo yis// til gyi gang bu bzhin du khyab// ston pa'i khyad 
3a5(rgyud 'grel): par yin par grags// gnas ni rnam pa gsum du grags// chos kyi dbyings dang gzhal yas khang // ba kha chos 'byung zhes su bya// mtha' dbus med pa chos kyi dbyings// de ni gnas kyi bla mar 'dod// gzhal yas bzhi dang 
3a6(rgyud 'grel): rgyu dang rgya// dbyibs dang blo 'bungar rtse mo dang // rgyan dang sgo khyud rta babs dang // mtshan nyid gdan gyi rnam pa ste// bcu gcig dag gis rnam par dbye'o// gzhi yang tshad med 'khor lo ste// ye shes lnga yi rang bzhin yin// ye shes/ 
3a7(rgyud 'grel): phyogs pan dbus brtags pas// rin chen las byas gzhal yas khang // ni krung yo bu ma byas pa// chos dbyings mtha' la khyab par snang // rgyas par rgyas byir gru bzhi papo// kun las spags pa'i gzungs bzhi dang // ye shes/ 
3a8(rgyud 'grel): bzhi'i ngo bo nyid// gcig la'ang ye shes kun gnas dang // gzhal byas mdzes par byas pa'i phyir// glo 'bur bzhi yang mkhar thabs tshul// bum pa'i rtse mo chos kyi rtog/ chos kyi dbyings su kun nas gnas// glo 'bur lnga'i 
3b1(rgyud 'grel): brgyad rnams kyang // dbyibs dang kha dog bye brag dag/ rigs kyi khyad par gyis ni dbye// gnas mchog nyid kyi rgyan mchog kyang // gzugs sgra dri ro reg gi rnams// rigs kyi khyad par gyis ni brtag/ so sor ma bsgrib 
3b2(rgyud 'grel): rang gis gsal// bar chad med par phyogs bcur 'khrigs// stong smon mtshan med 'od gsal 'jug/ de phyir ye shes sgo khyud can// nyan thos rang rgyal byang chub dang // bya ba rgyud dang gnyis ga rgyud// rnal 'byor skyed dang 
3b3(rgyud 'grel): rdzogs pa yi// rnam thar brgyad phyir rta babs brgyad// gnas mchog mtshan nyid brjod pa ni// gzhal yas phyi dang chos dbyings nang // bdag nyid du ni bsdus pas na// kun du nang zhes bshad pa yin// de na gnas pa'i 
3b4(rgyud 'grel): gdan mchog kyang // seng ge glang chen rta dang khyud// na mkha' lding gi khri chen la// nyi zla pad+ma rin po che// lnga rtsegs nyi shu rtsa lngar ldan// rgyal po rgyal mo'i gdan mchog la// mi 'jigs bzhi dang stobs bcu dang // rdzu 'phrul 
3b5(rgyud 'grel): bzhi dang dbang rnams bcu// thogs med 'phrin las rnam bzhi'o// thabs dang shes rab 'od gsal bar// skyon gyis ma gos zad mi shes// sngon sangs rgyas dang zag pa zad// bar mi chod dang nges par 'byung // 'jig rten 
3b6(rgyud 'grel): 'jig rten 'das bcas la// 'jigs med pa'i sems kyis su// chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor// gnas dang gnas min yang dag mkhyen// dus gsum las 'das rnam smin mkhyen// khams rnams sna tshogs mkhyen pa 
3b7(rgyud 'grel): dang // pha rol mos pa mkhyen pa'i stobs// dbang po mchog dang mchog min mkhyen// kun du 'gro lam mkhyen pa'i stobs// bsam gtan thar dang nyon mongs mkhyen// sngon gyi gnas mkhyen stobs dang ni// skye dang 'chi 
3b8(rgyud 'grel): 'pho mkhyen pa dang // zag pa zad med sems grol mkhyen// de bcu stobs bcur gyur pas na// 'bras bu sngon shes drug yin no// 'dun dang brtson 'grus sems dang ni// spyod pa'i ting 'dzin spong ba yin// 'du byed 
4a1(rgyud 'grel): rnams te rkang pa bzhi// ye shes pazhi grub 'bras bu ste// chos dbyings ye shes kun la khyab// yo byad skye ba tshol dbang // ye shes chos dang sems dang las// rdzu 'phrul smon lam mos rnams kyi/ 
4a2(rgyud 'grel): khams kun gyis ni dbang phyug rgyal// ni rgyas dbang drag las rnams kyis// thog med las rnams ldan gyis grub// ci la thogs pa med par spyod// gnas mchog khyad par de nyid kyang // dpyid phyug bkar bstan pa 
4a3(rgyud 'grel): yin// 'khor rnams bkod pa ji snyed pa// khams dang skye mched yin par grags// rnam shes yul deng dbang po dang // dus dang phyin ci ma log rnams// byang chub chen po'i rang bzhin du// lhun gyi grub pa'i dkyil 'khor
4a4(rgyud 'grel): yin// mthong dang thos dang snoms dang myong // rnam shes bzhi po sems dpar shar// mthong bya zos bya sdoms bya dang // myong bya 'dod pa'i lha mo rnams// rnam shes bzhi dang dbyer med par// mdzes pa'i blo 'bur ba ni
4a5(rgyud 'grel): pol// nyi zla pad+ma rin chen gdan// mthong byed zos byed snyoms byed dang // myong byed dbang po'i sems dpa' dang // 'das dang da ltar byung 'ong dang // 'byung bar ma nges lha mo bzhi// dbyer med tshul du grwa bzhir gnas// 
4a6(rgyud 'grel): reg pa reg byed reg bya dang // yid kyi khams te 'joms byed dang // rtag chad badrag tu ma yin dang // mtshan ma ma yin 'joms pa rnams// sgo bzhi phyogs su de bzhin gnas// kun bzang yid kyi rnam shes dang // chos ni 
4a7(rgyud 'grel): bya ba kun du bzang // mdun dang rgyab du rnam par gnas// de nyid bsdad pa phun sum tshogs// bsdu bya'i yul ni tshes yin te// byed pa po ni kun tu bzang // thugs kyi thugs te thugs yin no// srid gsum 'gro ba thams 
4a8(rgyud 'grel): cad kyis// phung po khams dang skye mched dag/ brjod med brjod kyis mi langs pa// de snyed 'khor lo dkyil 'khor du// sngoran rdzogs rgyal po de nyid nges// gnyis med lhun grub dkyil 'khor na// thams cad bdag nyid rtag tu 
4b1(rgyud 'grel): bzhugs// de nas ston pa bde gshegs rnams// btsun mo'i tshigs dang gnyis med pa'i// gsang ba mchog gi dkyil 'khor rnams// rgyad 'di nyid kyi mdo don ste// dkyil 'khor kun gyi gsang ba 'di// sku gsung yod 
4b2(rgyud 'grel): tan 'grin las thugs// rdo rje las ni nges par byang // ngo mtshar dkyil 'khor brjod pa'i tshig/ e zhes bya ba dam pa'i don// e ma zhes bya ba rab tu ngam// e ma ho zhes bya shin tu ngam// dkyil 'khor rnam pa bcu gnyis te// 
4b3(rgyud 'grel): de bzhin nyid dang rang bzhin dang // thugs rjes 'dul ba'i dkyil 'khor dang // ting nge 'dzin dang gzugs brnyan dang // lhag pa'i ting 'dzin gzugs brnyan dang // byang chub sems dang lhag byang sems// tshogs dang lhun grub 
4b4(rgyud 'grel): dkyil 'khor ro// chos kyi dbyings nyid de bzhin nyid// ye shes kyis ni dbang sgyur ba// rang bzhin thabs kyis dkyil 'khor nyid// thugs rje 'byung ba thugs rje'o// de nyid thugs rjes 'dul ba'i ngang // rang snang dbyer med dkyil 
4b5(rgyud 'grel): 'khor du// ting nge 'dzin gyis rnam par bsgom// rten 'byung mtshon par byed pas ra// gzugs brnyan sgyu ma'i dkyil 'khor ni// sgyu ma yin zhes rgyal bas gsungs// mkha' dbyings gsal bar rnams spyad pas// de yang rang 
4b6(rgyud 'grel): snang zhes su bshad// sku gsung yon tan 'phrin las thugs// de nyid mtshon pa'i thabs tshul du// sa la sogs la phyag rgya byas// lhag pa'i gzugs brnyad yin par grags// dam pa'i don gyi byang chub sems// til babru 
4b7(rgyud 'grel): bzhin ni kun la khyab// a'i po de rab tu bsdus// byang chub rdo rje dri las byung // lhag pa yid bzhin rin po che// sku gsung thugs ni mi zad pa// gter ldan brgyan gyi 'khor lo nyid// tshogs chen rdzogs pa ces su bshad// chos/ 
4b8(rgyud 'grel): sku rdo rje mchog nyid do// ma bcos lhun grub bdag nyid do// mnyam nyid dbyings kyi de bzhin nyid// man zhes bya ba snying po'i don// de la zhes bya len pa'o// yul dang dbang po yin par dgongs// spyod yul kun du maN+Dal// 
5a1(rgyud 'grel): rdo rje gsang bas gsungs pa dang // brjod dka' de nyid brjod pas na// rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig du'o// brjod du med pa'i ngo bo nyid// tshig du brjod pa ma yin yang // 'dzub mo sgron ma zla ba gser// don
5a2(rgyud 'grel): mtshon tshig ni don dang 'dra// don ni mi rtogs med min pa'o// dbul po'i gter dang gyad nor 'dra// tshig ni me long sgron ma'i tshul// 'gro ba'i don la brjod par bshad// des na bde gshegs rgyal ba rnams// nyid las 
5a3(rgyud 'grel): nyid kyis gsung mod kyi// 'gro la phan pa'i don gyi phyir// brjod pa nyid du rgyal bas gsung // gleng bzhi'i le'u ste dang po'o// / de nas ston pa rgyal mchog gis// dkyil 'khor mdo'i don gleng pa// de nyid don 'di bsdus
5a4(rgyud 'grel): 'dod nas// yab yum gnyis po gleng ba yin// yab kyi ye shes don rmongs pa// gang gis ji ltar gang glengs dang // glengs pa'i 'bras bu nyid dang bzhi// thams cad kun gyi byed pa po// kun bzang yid nyid rdo rje re// 
5a5(rgyud 'grel): ye shes rdo rje 'dul ba'i tshul// rang rig dbyings la 'jug 'gyur te// srid dang rnam grol thams cad kun// thig le'i tshul du dbyer med pas// ston pa rdo rje bde gshegs la// kun bzang bde bar gshegs nyid kyis/ 
5a6(rgyud 'grel): 'gro ba'i mched du 'di skad brjod// rang gi 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor la// ngo mtshar gyis ni tshig brjod de// srid dang rnam grol thams cad kyi// phung po'i yan lag rnam pa lnga// chos su rdo rje yin pa'i phyir// rgyal po lngaru 
5a7(rgyud 'grel): rnam par grags// 'gro ba'i 'gro ba thams cad kyi// khams dang skye mched rnam pa kun// sems pa sems ma'i dkyil 'khor yin// khams lnga dbyings phyug rgyal mo lnga// mdor na srid gsum thams cad kun/ 
5a8(rgyud 'grel): mngon rdzogs rgyal por de nyid nges// 'di skad tshig du gleng ba'i tshe// rgyal ba rigs lnga'i dkyil 'khor rnams// 'gro ba'i ched du mnyes gyur nas// yum gyi dbyings kyi don glengs pa// gang gis ji ltar ji skad glengs// 
5b1(rgyud 'grel): glengs pa'i 'bras bu nyid dang bzhi// bya ba mo ni kun du bzang // ye shes la ni dbyings phyag 'gyur// 'gro ba'i mched du gleng ba ni// stong gsum rdul snyed phyogs bcu kun// dngos por ma grub ye nas dbyen// srid gsum 
5b2(rgyud 'grel): 'gro ba'i gnas nyid las// zhing khams dag las gud na med// nyon mongs dus cho lta ba sems can nyid// snyigs ma lnga po 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal ste// bde chen gnas nyid las ni gzhan ma yin// nye bar len pa'i phung po 
5b3(rgyud 'grel): lnga po las// bde gshegs gud na yod ma yin// de bas thams cad snying po'i mchog/ gzhan du sangs rgyas rtsal ma yin// de skad tshig du glengs pa'i tshe// bde chen dbyings su sangs rgyas par// ston brgyal mchog 
5b4(rgyud 'grel): nyid kyis mkhyen// de nas rgyal po rdzogs sangs rgyas// btsun mo'i tshigs dang gnyis med pas// rnam gnyis glengs don thugs chung ste// gzhung don rnam pa bshad pa mdzad// rdzogs chen rtogs pa'i rnal 'byor pas// 
5b5(rgyud 'grel): rtogs spyod rnam pa nyi shu yis// mngon rdzogs rgyal por de nyid nges// byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed pa// thog mar 'gro ba'i lam mchog yin// byang chub mchog ldan rnal 'byor des// chos kun nges don gtan la 
5b6(rgyud 'grel): pag// nges pa'i don nyid rtogs pa'i tshe// ming tsam snang ba'i chos rnams kun// yi ge 'khor lo mngon sangs rgyas// mngon rdzogs yi ge de nyid las// ting 'dzin rol mo mtha' yas 'phros// spros nyid dkyil 'khor bsam 
5b7(rgyud 'grel): yas gsal// gsal byed sngags kyi yi ge brjod// de nyid thugs rtags phyag rgyar gsal// ma mthong sdongs la bstan pa'i phyir// bkri dang rdul tshon bstan pa ces// dkyil 'khor dag la brten pa'i mi// dbang mchog 
5b8(rgyud 'grel): sbyin pa mchog yin no// dbang mchog rdzogs nas tshogs la 'jug/ tshogs bsgrub yon tan bsam mi khyab// tshogs mchog rgya cher spel ba yang // man ngag snying po can gyis bya// tshogs dus stod pa glu yis bya// 
6a1(rgyud 'grel): gal te zhi bas mi 'dul na// rdo rje khro bo'i dkyil 'khor spro// khros pa'i sngags kyi bskur ston nas// dkyil 'khor nyid du bkod par bya// de nyid la ni mchod pa 'bul// zhi khro rab 'byam mchod pa'i tshe// 
6a2(rgyud 'grel): sdom la gnas pa shin tu gces// dam tshig ldan pa'i skyes bu de// rnam bzhi las kyi gzhan don bya// khros pa'i glu'i bstod pa bya// don dam kun rdzob byang chub sems// rnam pa gnyis su ston pas gsung // rmad du 
6a3(rgyud 'grel): byung ba'i byang chub sems// sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba'i thugs// ye shes lnga'i rang bzhin ni// skye 'gag gnas dmigs 'gro 'ong rnams// don dam med las kun sgrib yod// don dam kun sgrib dbyer med don// dam pa'i 
6a4(rgyud 'grel): don du bde gshegs gsungs// brjod med de nyid brjod pa'i tshe// nyid kyi rtse bzungs 'khor lo mnyes// don ma rdzogs dang snying rje dang // don mdzad kun rdzob rnam pa gsum// rgyal po rgyal mo 'khor bcas pas// rtogs 
6a5(rgyud 'grel): dka' gsang ba rnam bzhir brjod// ye nas rtogs dka'i gsang ba dang // sna tshogs chos rnams thams cad kyi// rang bzhin de nyid gsang ba dang // rang rang chos kyi ngo bo nyid// mtshan nyid so so rtogs pa gsang / 
6a6(rgyud 'grel): snod mir gzhan la mi bstan gsang // ma rtogs don nyid brjod pa yin// chos kun rang bzhin sangs rgyas kyang // de nyid ma rtogs 'khrul 'khor khyab// zhen pa bzlog phyir snying rje bskyed// rang bzhin gsang ba bstan pa'i phyir// 
6a7(rgyud 'grel): chos spobs pa yas spros pa mdzad// rang bzhin med pa'i chos nyid las// 'gro ba 'khrul 'khor snang ba yang // bdag 'dzin tsam las ma rtogs pa// 'khrul 'khor dngos nyid gal yod// dper na mkha' la mdud 
6a8(rgyud 'grel): 'dor 'dra// bdag 'dzin 'ching bdam po yang // bcings byed bcing brag la yod// de bas spun grub dkyil 'khor che// de nyid bstan phyir bshad pa mdzad// de skad bde gshegs rgyal mchog gis// 'khong rnams 
6b1(rgyud 'grel): bde gshegs dkyil 'khor la// 'gro ba rnams kyi mched du gsung // sems bskyed pa'i le'u ste// gnyis pa'o// // bstan la dbab par bya ba dang // bstan la phab pa gnyis su bshad// dbab bya sbrul skus 'dul bstan 
6b2(rgyud 'grel): la// nges pa'i don gyi bstan la phebs ces bya// gang las gang 'dzin gang du ci byed dang // gang gis don mdzad yin te rnam pa lnga'o// gang las rgyal mchog sku gsung las// thugs rje rig pa'i thub drug mthon// gang du las 
6b3(rgyud 'grel): kyi 'bras bu ste// stong gsum cig la chags tshul drug/ sprul skra cig gi zhing du grags// drug gi 'jig rten de nyid na// gling rnams bye ba phrag brgya yin// sprul pa bye ba phrag brgyar snang // gling rnams re rer sprul pa re rer yang // 
6b4(rgyud 'grel): 'gro drug las kyi drug du snang ba yin// dper na bar snang tha ba cig shar bas// 'dzam bu gling gi chu rnams kun du ru thar snang // chu cig nang na snang ba'i tha ba yang // 'gro ba so sos bltas na rang re'i mdun na snang // de bzhin sprul sku 
6b5(rgyud 'grel): cig la gling rnams snang // gling rnams cig las 'gro ba drug du snang // tha dad de kun sprul pa cig du grags// de 'dra'i stong gsum mtha' yas mu med na// de 'dra'i sprul pa re res 'gro don de ltar mdzad// ci mdzad 'dul ba rnam pa 
6b6(rgyud 'grel): bzhis// gang gis 'gro balnga don mdzad// mngon gsum rdzu 'phrul bsod nams rig pa bzhis// theg lnga'i rigs can 'gro lnga'i don rnams mdzad// mngon gsum 'dul bas sangs rgyas mdzad pa ston// rdzu 'phrul mthun 
6b7(rgyud 'grel): mangs ma yin rnon shes drug/ bsod nams kun du skang nga gsung thugs nas// bsam gyis mi khya grangs med phyogs bcung ldeng // rigs pas cig dang brgya bcur pa zhir gsungs pa// 'dul ba'i dbang gcig pa'i rigs 
6b8(rgyud 'grel): dang sbyar// nyon mongs rten por sgo mang dus gsum gsungs// gzugs 'dzin gyi nang rten 'brel 'dul rnams la// mi dang lga dang nyan thos rang rgyal bstan// 'khrul 'dogs las 'bras chud mi zas 'dul lo// byang chub 
7a1(rgyud 'grel): sems dpa'i theg pas pan 'dogs so// las 'bras mi tshigs rtogs pa'i thosngon pa// tha med rdo rje theg pa'i mthar thug/ de kun 'dul ba'i dbang sde ba'i ba'i don// de dag nges par bstan 
7a2(rgyud 'grel): la dbab pa yang // bde gshegs rgyal bas 'gro ba'i ched brjod pa// lha mi nyan thos rang rgyal theg pa le// mi rigs gzugs 'dzin gyi nang rten 'brel 'khor// mi mthun pa de dang sdug bsngal sa chags kyang // 'phrul pa 'i/ 
7a3(rgyud 'grel): snang ba ma gtogs par// rang bzhin dbyings las nyams pa med ces gsung // bden pa gnyis rtogs byang chub sems dpa' yang // gnyis tshul bdag dang bdag gis gzhan med de// rnam dag chos kyi dbyings las gnyis su med// 
7a4(rgyud 'grel): bdag gzhan rtog pa tsam ste don du med// log rgyud nyid rtog rang sems skad cig ma// skad cig gzhi rtsa med par chos kyi dbyings// bla med dngos grub gzhan nas re ba yang // bdag dang gzhan du rtog pa'i rgyun yin pas// 
7a5(rgyud 'grel): nyid la nyid spyod nyid la nyid dbang bskur// theg po'i khyad par rnam lngar bstan pa yang // 'bras bu rdzogs chen theg pa cig tu gnas// bsod nams bsam gyis mi khyab snang ba dang // khyad par sngon shes drug du snang ba yang // 
7a6(rgyud 'grel): bsod nams rgyu las grub pa ma yin te// de nyid yang dag rtogs pa'i byin rlabs las// rang bzhin med las cir yang grub// sangs rgyas mdzad pa rims par ston pa yang // 'gro ba 'dul ba'i thabs las ma rtogs pa// 
7a7(rgyud 'grel): sangs rgyas zhes bya mya ngan ci la 'da'// chos kyi dbyings kyang nub par mi 'gyur ro// 'di skad bshad pa zhes kyang de phyir brjod// zhing khams kun du grags pa'i snying po 'di// sde snod kun dang rgyud kun 'byung ba'i yum// de phyir 
7a8(rgyud 'grel): snying po zhes su rgyal bas gsungs// de dag bstan la 'bebs pas nges dbang yin// de phyir bstan pa yongs kyi 'byung gnas yin// nyon mongs brgyad khri bzhi stong snyen po ru// ming dang tshig du sgo rnams bstan pa 
7b1(rgyud 'grel): yang // 'gro ba 'dul ba'i dbang tsam ma rtogs pa// ston ming tshig la dngos po ga la yod// de kun tha snyad yin zhes rgyal bas ched du brjod// de nas nyid kyi gsang ba yi// dkyil 'khor kun gyi gsang ba 'di// sku 
7b2(rgyud 'grel): gsung rdo rje nyid las byung // a ni skyed med shes rab dbyings// ho ni thabs mchog cho 'phrul rol// srid gsum 'khrul 'khor thams cad kun// log rtog nyid las ci yang min// log rtog bzhi rtsa med dbyings yin// rang rig 
7b3(rgyud 'grel): ye shes bdag med thugs// bya byed med pas kun dbang bsgyur// de nyid yon tan zhing khams las// gzhan med rang rig de ltar snang // rdul snyed sprul pa bsam yas kyis// 'dul ba'i dbang gis gsungs pa kun// / 
7b4(rgyud 'grel): bla med nges pa'i don 'di ru// 'dus par bde gshegs nyid kyis mkhyen// bstan la bab pa'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// // yi ge 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor 'di// gang las ji ltar gang phyung phyung ba'i 'bru// don bshad 
7b5(rgyud 'grel): gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor phyung ba dang // rnam pa 'di drug yi ge 'khor lo bshad// gang las byung ba rnam bzhir shes bya ste// dgongs dang ting 'dzin ming dang 'byung khung so// bde gshegs mnyam nyid dgongs pa gcig tu gyur// 
7b6(rgyud 'grel): mnyam nyid rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor du// chos kun ye nas sangs rgyas ting 'dzin bstan// kun rdzob ming tsam yi ge 'phreng zhes bya// byung khungs ston pa'i sku gsung thugs rdo rje// ji ltar a b+hung a las ming tshogs 
7b7(rgyud 'grel): byung // a dkar bzhi las a rnams phyogs bcur 'phros// phyogs kun gsal nas slar 'dus gzhi la thims// 'phros pas 'grib med sdus pas 'phel med pa// spros pas gzhan don sdus pas bdag gi don// a 'dar 
7b8(rgyud 'grel): ka la sogs pa bzhi bcu gnyis// shin tu phra ba'i tshul gyi spro bsdu ba// mi 'grib mi 'phel bdag gzhan don du bshad// a nyid rgyu ste ming tshigs 'bras bur gsungs// sku gsung thugs kyi glong nas a 'byung ste// a ni khongs 
8a1(rgyud 'grel): nas 'bung bas skye ba med// a las 'od zer 'gur gyi gsang bar 'khyil// 'od 'phros ka la sogs pa 'bru lngar shar// a'i 'od zer zla kham ljags la 'khyil// 'od 'phros rtsa la sogs pa 'bru lngar shar/ 
8a2(rgyud 'grel): a'i 'od zer ljags kyi rtser 'phros pas// cho 'phrul ta la sogs pa 'bru ba cur shar// zhal gyi sgo mor a'i 'od 'phros pas// cho 'phrul pa la sogs pa 'bru lnga yin// a las phyi rol yul la 'od 'phros pas// 
8a3(rgyud 'grel): cho 'phrul yi ge nyi shu sku las 'phros// ya ni byin pa las byung wa ni sku khab las// ra ni rtag zur la ni dpungs pa las ni byung // thugs kha'i 'od las sha byung phyag 'thil las ni Sha// mdzod spu 'od las sa 
8a4(rgyud 'grel): byung zhabs 'thil gnyis las ha// gsang ba'i 'od zer las ni cho 'phrul kA ru shar// lhan gnyis las ni cho 'phrul i gnyis shar// stan gnyis las ni cho 'phrul u gnyis shar// tshems gnyis las ni 'od 'gros 
8a5(rgyud 'grel): oM gnyis shar// shangs gnyis las ni 'od 'phros oM gnyis shar// skyes bu'i spyi gtsug 'od 'phros mgo zhes bya zer// 'khru chad lte ba las ni 'od 'phros shad ces bya// skyes bu chen po 'tshogs ma'i 'od las 
8a6(rgyud 'grel): thig ces bya// gar byung bzhi bcu rtsa lnga de nyid yin// phyung ba'i nus 'bru 'jig rten bsam yas g.yo// don bshad rnam pa gnyis su shes bya ste// spyi dang rang gi mtshan nyid don bshad pa'o// spyi'i don ni rnam// 
8a7(rgyud 'grel): dgur shes bya ste// don dang che ba las dang mtshan nyid drangs// dbye ba rang bzhin cho 'phrul nges tshig go// don ni bden pa gnyis su zhes bya ste// an don dam mtha' gnyis dbus mi dmigs// kun rdzob ming tsam 
8a8(rgyud 'grel): yig 'phreng ba nyid// chos kun sum ming tsam nyid la gnas// a las yiga'i tshogs 'byung sgra dang bcas// snyid tsam tshig gi bsdus pa'i mngon rdzogs nyid// rdzogs sangs rgyas te yi ge'i tsho bar gsungs// 
8b1(rgyud 'grel): las ni ya mtshan bzhi bcu rtsa lnga yis// ming tshig don mtshon sna tshogs smra zhing ston// mtshan nyid don dam dbyings las dmigs med kyang // kha dog ming dbyibs rol pa sprul cing ston// rnam grangs dkyil 
8b2(rgyud 'grel): 'khor bzhi bcu rtsa lnga nyid// re re la yang sku gsung thugs su bshad// thugs ni hUM nyid a yis kun la khyab// sku ni so so'i kha dog dbyibs su ldan// gsung ni sgra yi ming gis thams cad bsdus// de phyir 
8b3(rgyud 'grel): phyogs bcur rgyal ba'i sku gsung thugs// bzhi bcu rtsa lnga gsum 'gror 'gyur zhes gsung // dbye ba lus dang yan lag gnyis su dbye// lus ni mgo nas kwa'i bar du rdzogs// yan lag 'drin dang grag po 
8b4(rgyud 'grel): bzhi gnyis yin// rang bzhin sems nyid yi ge'i rang bzhin ste// sems dang yi ge'i dngos po yod ma yin// cho 'phrul mtshan ma dbyings las sna tshogs sprul// rgyal ba'i sku gsung thugs kyi cho 'phrul 
8b5(rgyud 'grel): rnams// yi ge mthu'i 'gug cing byed nus na// 'jig rten cho 'phrul gzhan lta smos ci dgos// nges tshig bris pa'i phyir na yi ge ste// mtshan med dbyings la dbyings kyi bris pa yang // a nyid dbyings 
8b6(rgyud 'grel): las sna tshogs 'byung phyir ro// rang gi mtshan nyid so sor bshad pa ni// bzhi bcu rtsa drug rang bzhin las rnams yin// mgo'i rang bzhin ma nor de nyid rnam pa gsum// las ni lam yin rtog pa rnam pa bzhi// 
8b7(rgyud 'grel): thig gi rang bzhin shes rab rnam pa gsum// las ni de nyid mtshon byed ming du smra// shad ni rang bzhin thabs chen snyan bsgrub bzhi// las ni mtshon pa'i ming rnams tshig su gcod// a'i rang bzhin skye med dbu ma'i dang // 
8b8(rgyud 'grel): las ni de bzhin nyid mtshon dag mnyam bzhi// a mgo thig bshad ting 'dzin bzhir bshad de// de bzhin nyid kun snang sna rdzogs zhes bya// des na sngon rdzogs phyag rgya'i rgyu bzhir nges// tha sogs bde gshegs 
9a1(rgyud 'grel): lnga rdzogs phung po lnga'i// rang bzhin sgyu 'phrul yin te las ni rigs lnga'o// tha sogs lnga ni btsun mo'i dbyings rnams lnga// rang bzhin dra ba las ni 'byung lnga nyid// sgyu 'phrul dra ba zhes kyang 
9a2(rgyud 'grel): dang gzungs la grags// ka la sogs pa sems dpa'i yi ge lnga// rang bzhin thugs ste les ni rnam shes khams lnga yin// tsa sogs yul gyi sems bzhi rigs dang rnams lnga po// rang bzhin sku ste las ni yul 
9a3(rgyud 'grel): gyi khams lnga yin// sa la sogs pa sems dpa'i yi ge lnga'o// rang bzhin gsungs te las ni dbang po'i khams lnga yin// yal sogs pa reg ma'i yi ge bzhi// rang bzhin dag pa bzhi ste las ni dus rnams bzhi/ 
9a4(rgyud 'grel): sha la sogs pa rigs ma'i yi ge bzhi// rang bzhin med pa bzhi ste las ni mtha' bzhi 'joms// k+ka ni sdus pa'i rang bzhin thugs kyi thugs ste las ni ye shes yin// i la sogs pa sprul pa'i yi ge rnams drug go/ 
9a5(rgyud 'grel): sprul pa'i rang bzhin bsam yas rdul snyed las ni rigs drug 'dul// oM ni yid dbang rig pa'i rgyal po'i yi ge ste// rang bzhin byang chub sems ste las ni thams cad 'jig/ oM ni sdud bya kun tu bzang mo'i yi 
9a6(rgyud 'grel): gi ste// rang bzhin chos rnams thams cad las ni kun bzhi yin// las dang rang bzhin 'brel pa'i 'khor lo'i tshogs chen 'di// re re la yang sku gsung thugs kyi man Da la rdzogs pa'i 'phreng // yi ge 'khor la
9a7(rgyud 'grel): tshegs chen zhes su brjod// yig 'bru gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor ni// gang byung gang las ji ltar byung // byung ba'i 'bras bu nyid dang bzhi// gang byung ba der gshegs thams cad kyi// rab tu gsang ba'i dkyil
9a8(rgyud 'grel): 'khor yin// gang las sku gsung rdo rje las// ji ltar yab yum dgyes sprin las// ar gsal a las yig 'bru tshogs// de la sngon rdzogs skur gsal ba// yum gyi mkha' la rdzogs par rel// lhag 
9b1(rgyud 'grel): pa'i ting 'dzin zhes su grags// de nyid las ni phyi rol gyi// dkyil 'khor 'don par rgyal bas gsungs// b+ha ga dkyil 'khor ling ka a// 'dul ma byas nyid rdo rje las// 'dus byas rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor tshogs// 
9b2(rgyud 'grel): 'byin pa'i dam tshig 'da' mi 'gyur// ci phyir thabs dang shes rab kyi// rgyu rkyen tshogs pa'i thu chen yin// de'i 'bras bu yi ge nyid// rgyal ba mngon par rdzogs pa'i sku// dkyil 'khor nyid du ldan gyis grub/ 
9b3(rgyud 'grel): yi ge 'phreng ba bkod pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// // sna tshogs sgyu 'phrul spros pa 'di// gang las gang spros thabs dang mnyes pa bzhi// gang las sgyu 'phrul dkyil 'khor bkod pa las// gang spros te nge 'dzin rnam 
9b4(rgyud 'grel): par spros pa 'di// thabs ni bdun gyis bsgrub thabs sdebs bshad pa// ting nge 'dzin dang rdzogs dang thun mong dang // dper dang sgra dang gags gsal mchog rdzogs 'gyur// ting 'dzin de bzhin nyid dang kun snang 
9b5(rgyud 'grel): sgra yin te// ting 'dzin de bzhin rang sems mtshan nyid ni// gang gis mi shes chos kyi dbyings mi shes// dmigs med mi shes rtag chad 'jig mi 'gyur// de phyir rang sems dbyings nyid thabs kyi rgyu// dngos 
9b6(rgyud 'grel): pa rnam pa brgyad sogs gang yang min// min pa de nyid de bzhin nyid ces bya// de nyid gsal bar sgom pa thabs kyi rgyu// kun khyab snying rje rang bzhin kun snang yin// rgyu ni sems nyid a'i rang bzhin ste// a nyid 
9b7(rgyud 'grel): yid bzhin rin chen sprin dang mtshungs// a las sgyu 'phrul bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis 'byung // de nyid thabs las thabs byung thabs bsam yas// thabs nyid dra ba'i dkyil 'khor rdzogs pa'i sku// rdzogs pa'i yig 'bru 
9b8(rgyud 'grel): phyag mtshan sngon rdzogs sku// don dam dbyer med kun rdzob tha dad pa'i// nang gi rnam shes nang gi dbang po dang // phyi rol yul gyi rnam pa thams cad kun// bsam yas dkyil 'khor kun bzang phyag rgyar rol// 
10a1(rgyud 'grel): de nyid sgyu 'phrul mngon rdzogs rgyal por nges// dngos grub thun mongs rnam pasna chags kun// glang chen byos 'dra'i sems ni ting nge 'dzin gyi btul nas su// sku 'phrul sngags dang phyag rgya rab tu 
10a2(rgyud 'grel): bstan byas nas// thun mongs dngos grub ya mtshan 'di kun 'grub// phyogs dus rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor grub nas rgyal ba'i dpal// nyi shu rtsa gcig ting 'dzin mthu yis grub// dper na sgron ma gser 'gyur sman gyi 
10a3(rgyud 'grel): dug gsel dang // zangs las gser 'gyur dug las sman 'gyur ltar// ye shes rang snang ming tshig gzugs sogs las// yid bzhin dngos grub ji ltar skur bas 'grub// bla ma mchod ldan rtogs gsal dam tshig ldan// 
10a4(rgyud 'grel): sngags shes phyag rgyar shes shing yo byad lnga ldan na// thun mongs mchog gi dngos grub yod par rgyal bas gsung // de nyid mi ldan dngos grub med de de nyid drug par 'gyur// de dag thob pa'i rgyu dang mi thob gags zhes bshad// 
10a5(rgyud 'grel): mchog de nyid ni rgyal ba'i thugs chung dngos grub snying po ste// mi zad 'phel 'grib med pa yid bzhin mdzod dang 'dra// dngos med ting nge 'dzin las dngos po yi ge sprin// mchog gi rnam pa sna tshogs ji ltar 'dod 
10a6(rgyud 'grel): 'byung 'gyur// dngos med dngos nyid rtog pa'i ting 'dzin mchog gi mthus// dbang skur bder gshegs kun gyi bdag nyid de yin no// de skad gsung bas 'khor gyi bde gshegs thams cad kun// mchog dang thun 
10a7(rgyud 'grel): mang gzigs mos mnyes par 'gyur// sku 'phrul sgrub pa ting nge 'dzin gyi le'u ste lnga pa'o// // de nas rdzu 'phrul dkyil 'khor spros bshad pa// gang gis gang du gang spros ji ltar 'gyur// gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor 
10a8(rgyud 'grel): spros te rnam lnga yin// gang gis ston pa bde gshegs thams cad kyang // rang bzhin gcig dang du med bden gnyis dbyer med pas// gang du 'jig rten drug gi bsam yas thams cad la// rgyal ba nyid 
10b1(rgyud 'grel): kyi sku gsung che ba'i dkyil 'khor 'byin par dgongs// gang spros rtogs dang spyod pa gnyis su bshad// rtog pa ji ltar gang rtags gang gis rtags na don 'byung ba'o// de ltar phyogs bzhi dbus ltar ye shes 
10b2(rgyud 'grel): lngar rtags te// gang rtags bsam yas 'jig rten lhun grub nyid ni par// gang gis bde gshegs rdzogs pa rtog pa'i rnal 'byor bde gshegs mtshungs// brtags nas don 'byung kun 'byung dkyil 'khor 
10b3(rgyud 'grel): chen por spyod// mdzad spyod rnam pa bcu yis ldan gyis grub// gzhal yas brgyan dang gdan khri bzhugs tshul dang // bzhugs gnas thugs mtshan sku mdog tshul dgu dang // 'di zer 'gro dang khyab pa che bgro 
10b4(rgyud 'grel): gzhal yas 'khor 'khrud gr-i khyams gru ba'i sgo'i khyung bzhi// brgyan ni rol mo'i sprin bung lha mchog pa'i bcu gnyis sogs len// gdan mchog lnga rtsigs nyi shu rtsa lnga po// bzhugs tshul sangs rgyas rdzogs 
10b5(rgyud 'grel): dkyil byang chub sems dpa'i tshul// sprul pa gzhongs tshul sgo bsrungs stang stabs tshul// gnas ni 'khor lo rtsibs la rgyal po rgyal mo bcu// glo 'gur bzhil rigs bzhi yul bzhi zung bzhi 'khril// gra bzhir 
10b6(rgyud 'grel): dbang po bzhi dang dus bzhi zungs 'khril nas// 'khyams la thub drug bya byung nub dang shar// sgo bzhir 'joms pa 'joms ma de bzhin du// thugs mtshan rgyal po phyag drug phyag rngu drug/ drug lnga sum nu ye shes 
10b7(rgyud 'grel): rtags su bstan// rnam shes rdo rje ral gri 'khor lo ga yas// dril bu rin chen pad+ma g.yon na 'dzin// gzugs ni 'khor lo ral gri rdo rje g.yas// dril bu pad+ma rin chen g.yon na 'dzin// tshor ba rin chen 'khor 
10b8(rgyud 'grel): lo rdo rje g.yas// dril bu pad+ma ral grig yon na 'dzin/ 'du shes pad+ma 'khor la rdo rje g.yas// dril bu rin chen ral gri g.yon na 'dzin// 'du byed ral gri 'khor lo rdo rje g.yas// dril bu rin chen pad+ma g.yonan 
11a1(rgyud 'grel): 'dzin// rgyal mo g.yas kyi dang po dril bu ste// g.yon pa dang rtags bzhi bzhi rtsa dang 'thun// shes rab yum yang drug lnga sum nur bshad// ut+pal klu shing po ti pad+ma dkar// dri spos me tog mar me/ 
11a2(rgyud 'grel): dbang bzhi dus bzhi yin// shes bzhi myu gu ral gri pad+ma rdo rje dang // mdzes 'phreng gi bang gar ni yul bzhi'o// pi wang sreg par go cha po ti dang // rin chen sgom dang me chu thub par grags// mnyam bzhag ting 'dzin 
11a3(rgyud 'grel): phyag rgya yin chos yin// 'joms ni mgo dang thod sprul rdo rje rgya gram g.yon// lcags kyu zhags pa lcags sgrog dril 'joms mtshan// kun kyang zhal gcig phyag gnyis mdzes pa'i yo byad 'dzin// mdog ni rtso
11a4(rgyud 'grel): bzung rab rig kha dog lnga// gcig la yang lnga lnga nyi shu rtsa lngar brtags// thub drug mdog ni cis 'dul nges pa med// yid chos 'thing ka nam mkha'i mdog du bstan// gzhan rnams rigs kyi bye brag dag gis/ 
11a5(rgyud 'grel): dbye// tshul ni bsnyen lcags 'khril ldem gzhon chas can// gsal la 'tsher la ldan sdug gzi byin ldan// 'joms pa 'joms ma rtogs pa tshul dgu po// 'od zer 'khyil cing brgyan yang 'khyil pa ste// 'od zer// 
11a6(rgyud 'grel): lnga la nyi shu rtsa lngar 'phros shing 'khyil// stong rtsa lnga bcur phyogs bcur 'phros gyur kyang // stong phrag bcu dang brgya phrag lnga yin no// 'byung ba'i gnas kyi tha dad brtsis 'gyur na// bcu po gcig la'ang spyan drug 
11a7(rgyud 'grel): snyan drug ste// de bzhin shangs ljags sku dang thugs mtshan drug/ sum cu drug la nyi shu lnga lngar 'phros// spyir ni stong phrag dgu ni bshad pa yin// sum cu gnyis po gcig la'ang bcu dang gnyis// 
11a8(rgyud 'grel): de bzhin spros na stong dgu brgya phrag drug/ stong phrag bco brgyad brgya phrag drug ces bya// de las phyogs bcur spos na khri phrag ni// bco brgyad stong phrag drug du bshad pa yin// de ltar phyogs 
11b1(rgyud 'grel): bcur 'gro drug don byed tshe// bye ba khrag khrig drug cu 'phro zhing 'khyil// yan lag nyid lag tshul dgu'i brgyan rnams las// legs par rtsis na rtsi sa las 'das pa yin// dkyil 'khor bsam 
11b2(rgyud 'grel): yas zhes kyang de la bya// rgyan ni dbu brgyan snyan cha 'gur chu dpung brgyan dang // phyag rngub zhabs rngub sku rigs se mo do// rin chen rgyu las grub ste dbyings dang ye shes brgyan// bcu po dag la ya na/ 
11b3(rgyud 'grel): dbu brgyan rigs lnga ste// sum cu gnyis la bdag po re re yin// bcu po lnga ni snyan cha drug drug ste// gzhan yang gnyis gnyis 'gur chu gsum dang gcig/ dpung brgyan phyag rngub drug dang gnyis de 
11b4(rgyud 'grel): bzhin// kun la zhabs rngub gnyis gnyis brgyan par bshad// sku regs si ma do ni re re'o// bcu po re re la yang sum cu ste// gzhan dag la ni bcu dang gnyis kyis brgyan// spyir ni drug brgya dang ni brgya 
11b5(rgyud 'grel): bcu bzhi// des na brgyan gyi dkyil 'khor lhun gyis grub// khyab pa'i che ba nam mkhas gar khyab pa'i// bsam yas dkyil 'khor gyis ni khyab par grags// drug cu rtsa gnyis spyan gyis drug cu rtsa 
11b6(rgyud 'grel): gnyis mtha' la gzigs// de bzhin snyan rnams kyis ni drug cu rtsa gnyis mtha' gsan cing // shangs nas drug cu rtsa gnyis sprul pa 'gyed// ljags kyis drug cu rtsa gnyis rdul thabs 'chad// sku ni// 
11b7(rgyud 'grel): drug cu rtsa gnyis 'dul ba mdzad// thugs ni drug cu rtsa gnyis phyin ci ma log mkhyen// sum brgya bdun cu rtsa gnyis dgongs pa bas ma mi khyab// dkyil 'khor bas ma yas lhun grub ces kyang de 
11b8(rgyud 'grel): la bya'o// ji ltar gyur na 'di ltar spros pa'i tshe// 'jig rten mtha' yas mu med thams cad kun// rdul snyed brjod kyis mi lang dkyil 'khor rdzogs// khams gsum sems can gcig gis 
12a1(rgyud 'grel): rgyud la yang // de snyed dkyil 'khor bsam yas lhun gyis grub// ting 'dzin gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor spros pa yang // sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje nyid las 'byung // dkyil 'khor dmigs 
12a2(rgyud 'grel): par bya ba byed pa mi dmigs te// dpag cing bsam 'das brjod med dkyil 'khor de nyid rang rig yin// de nyid mnyam dang mi mnyam chos la khyab tsam nyid na khyab pa med// khyab med de nyid khyab pa'i

12a7(rgyud 'grel): sa ma ya oM ces pa la sogs pas bskul ba yin// dngos grub tshon tshig bshad sngags bcas brjod// rgyal ba'i sku gsung thugs dang yon tan dang // 'phrin las dag dang lnga po re re yang // rnam pa lnga lnga mkhas 
12a8(rgyud 'grel): bas bshad pa de// nyid rtogs dang bdag nyid mnyam par sbyor ba yin// sku lnga rmad du byung bar bstan pa ni// chos sku longs spyod rdzogs dang sprul sku dang // mngon par byang chub rdo rje'i sku dang lnga// rtag tu mkha' 
12b1(rgyud 'grel): 'dod bde spyod zas sbyin 'dod// mngon par byang chub lnga sogs 'dus ma byas// gsung lnga rmad du byung bar bstan pa ni// yi ge med rigs longs spyod rdzogs gsung dang // tshangs dbyangs yan lag gsungs dang

12b3(rgyud 'grel): thugs dang lnga// me long mi rtog kun mkhyen mnyam pa nyid// nan tan las te ma skyes chos kyi dbyings// yon tan rmad du byung ba lngar bstan pa// zhing khams gzhal yas 'od zer gdan khri dang // che ba'i longs spyod
12b4(rgyud 'grel): bsam gyis mi khyab pa// thugs rje sprul cing byams pa'i khyim du bsdud// btang snyoms gzer 'phros sgrib pasel yon tan brtags// khar zhugs dag pa lnga spyod re 'dod rkong // 'phrin las rmad du byung ba lngar bstan

12b6(rgyud 'grel): la'ang de ltar brtsis gyur na// thug pa med par mi zad brgyan du snang // rmad byung chen po zhes kyang de la bya'o// grags pas bsam yas gsung gi dkyil 'khor gyis// bsam yas dkyil 'khor dag du rab tu 
12b7(rgyud 'grel): grags// gsang ba'i dbang ni rnam pa bzhi yin te// gang gis gang zhig gang la ji ltar bskur// gang gis rgyal po rgyal mo rtse gzungs kyis// gsang ba de nyid thugs la bsdu bya'i phyir// gang zhig gis ni 
12b8(rgyud 'grel): lhag pa'i sbyor sems kyis// lha mo brgyad kyis sbyor ba brda' smos te// sa ma ya ste yum gyis bskul ba yin// bdag ni dam tshig bstan ma zhes ni de la bya// sa ma ya hi rtse bos lan byin te// khyod ni 
13a1(rgyud 'grel): dam tshig dga' ma zhes su bya// ra ho haM ni brtsol bskul ba ste// bdag ni chags pa can pas chags mdzod che'o// ra ga ya mi bskul ba'i lan yin te// khyod ni chags pas chags pa'i gnas 
13a2(rgyud 'grel): ces bya'o// smon dang 'jug dang ldangs dang gnas pa'i// byang chub rnam pa bzhir yang mkhas pas bshad// dzA ni lcags kyus gzungs nyid 'dren pa yin// hUM ni zhags pa'i phyag rgyas 'khyud pa mdzad// baM ni sgrog 
13a3(rgyud 'grel): ste dbang po bsdam pa yin// ho ni dril bus mnyes par byed pa'i brda'// phyag rgya bzhi zhes kyang ni mkhas pas bshad// pra be shas ni pad+ma'i sgo phye yin// a be shas ni 'bebs pa zhes su bshad// pu ke zhes bya bde
13a4(rgyud 'grel): bar rngar pa'o// tsit+ta byang chub sems kyi thig le nyid// g.yo dang / reg dang myongs dang / myongs zhes pa/ reg pa rnam pa bzhir yang mkhas pas bshad// gang la yid ches gtso gzungs de nyid la// ji ltar byang

13a6(rgyud 'grel): bzhin bstan te rnam pa bzhi// gang las sku gsung thugs kyi sgyu 'phrul las// ye shes lnga dang sku gsung thugs nyid dang // chags dang mchod pa byin rlobs snying po 'byung // ji ltar ye shes kyis ni thims par 'gyur/

13b1(rgyud 'grel): la bya// 'gro drug gcig la'ang sgra skad tha dad pas// bsam gyis mi khyab sgra skad tha dad grags// de phyir gsung gi dkyil 'khor mtha' yas mchog/ ces gsungs sngags kyi le'u ste bdun pa'o// // phyag
13b2(rgyud 'grel): rgya'i dkyil 'khor bshad bya ba// gang gis ji ltar gang gsungs pa// gang gis rgyal ba nyid kyis gsungs// ji ltar yan lag dkyil 'khor de// dbu ni bde gshegs rigs yin te// lag g.yas rdo rje mi bskyod pa//

13b4(rgyud 'grel): yum bcu// nyi zla'i 'od bkod 'bru byin rlabs// gung gnyis la ni hUM dang muM// 'dzub mo gnyis la oM dang lang // dbang po gnyis las dang maM// chung ngu l-i ni oM dang spyi// sbom po gnyis la ha dang taM// de ltar byin

14a1(rgyud 'grel): bla bsngal 'bru sras dril bsil rin chen rigs// 'khril tshul chos la brtan pa pad+ma'i rigs// de nyid byed pa las kyi rigs// yum yang thugs brtan bde bar gshegs pa'i rigs// dril bsil rdo rje
